</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">Design Cost-Optimized Architectures</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-wrapper--2bGiz"><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane--sIcOh result-pane--accordion-panel--TEJg7"><div class="result-pane--question-header-wrapper--3DCpC"><div class="result-pane--question-header--pTUOx"><span class="result-pane--question-header-collapsed-text--WVdEr"><span class="result-pane--pane-title--f-2kd ud-heading-md"><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon" class="result-pane--answer-status-icon--ebl6C"><span class="result-pane--question-icon-background--AskFJ" data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon-background" style="background: oklch(0.9759 0.0029 264.54);"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium" style="color: oklch(0.6671 0.2202 28.6);"><use xlink:href="#icon-error"></use></svg></span></span><span>Question 46</span><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-label" style="color: oklch(0.5573 0.2161 29.71);">Incorrect</span></span><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-large ud-btn-ghost ud-btn-text-md ud-btn-icon ud-btn-icon-large"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-collapse"></use></svg></button></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="result-pane--question-format--PBvdY ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="question-prompt"><p>The engineering team at an e-commerce company wants to migrate from Amazon Simple Queue Service (Amazon SQS) Standard queues to FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queues with batching.</p>


<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following steps would you have in the migration checklist? (Select three)</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Make sure that the name of the FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue is the same as the standard queue</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct selection</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Make sure that the throughput for the target FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue does not exceed 3,000 messages per second</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your selection is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-filled"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Make sure that the name of the FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue ends with the .fifo suffix</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your selection is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-wrong-selection"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Make sure that the throughput for the target FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue does not exceed 300 messages per second</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your selection is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-filled"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Delete the existing standard queue and recreate it as a FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Convert the existing standard queue into a FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1007">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct options:</p>


<p><strong>Delete the existing standard queue and recreate it as a FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue</strong></p>


<p><strong>Make sure that the name of the FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue ends with the .fifo suffix</strong></p>


<p><strong>Make sure that the throughput for the target FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue does not exceed 3,000 messages per second</strong></p>


<p>Amazon Simple Queue Service (SQS) is a fully managed message queuing service that enables you to decouple and scale microservices, distributed systems, and serverless applications. Amazon SQS eliminates the complexity and overhead associated with managing and operating message oriented middleware, and empowers developers to focus on differentiating work. Using Amazon SQS, you can send, store, and receive messages between software components at any volume, without losing messages or requiring other services to be available.</p>


<p>Amazon SQS offers two types of message queues. Standard queues offer maximum throughput, best-effort ordering, and at-least-once delivery. SQS FIFO queues are designed to guarantee that messages are processed exactly once, in the exact order that they are sent.</p>


<p>By default, FIFO queues support up to 3,000 messages per second with batching, or up to 300 messages per second (300 send, receive, or delete operations per second) without batching. Therefore, using batching you can meet a throughput requirement of upto 3,000 messages per second.</p>


<p>The name of a FIFO queue must end with the .fifo suffix. The suffix counts towards the 80-character queue name limit. To determine whether a queue is FIFO, you can check whether the queue name ends with the suffix.</p>


<p>If you have an existing application that uses standard queues and you want to take advantage of the ordering or exactly-once processing features of FIFO queues, you need to configure the queue and your application correctly. You can't convert an existing standard queue into a FIFO queue. To make the move, you must either create a new FIFO queue for your application or delete your existing standard queue and recreate it as a FIFO queue.</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Convert the existing standard queue into a FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue</strong></p>


<p><strong>Make sure that the name of the FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue is the same as the standard queue</strong> - The name of a FIFO queue must end with the .fifo suffix.</p>


<p><strong>Make sure that the throughput for the target FIFO (First-In-First-Out) queue does not exceed 300 messages per second</strong> - By default, FIFO queues support up to 3,000 messages per second with batching.</p>


<p>References:</p>

</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">Design Resilient Architectures</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-wrapper--2bGiz"><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane--sIcOh result-pane--accordion-panel--TEJg7"><div class="result-pane--question-header-wrapper--3DCpC"><div class="result-pane--question-header--pTUOx"><span class="result-pane--question-header-collapsed-text--WVdEr"><span class="result-pane--pane-title--f-2kd ud-heading-md"><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon" class="result-pane--answer-status-icon--ebl6C"><span class="result-pane--question-icon-background--AskFJ" data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon-background" style="background: oklch(0.9759 0.0029 264.54);"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium" style="color: oklch(0.6671 0.2202 28.6);"><use xlink:href="#icon-error"></use></svg></span></span><span>Question 47</span><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-label" style="color: oklch(0.5573 0.2161 29.71);">Incorrect</span></span><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-large ud-btn-ghost ud-btn-text-md ud-btn-icon ud-btn-icon-large"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-collapse"></use></svg></button></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="result-pane--question-format--PBvdY ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="question-prompt"><p>The business analytics team at a company has been running ad-hoc queries on Oracle and PostgreSQL services on Amazon RDS to prepare daily reports for senior management. To facilitate the business analytics reporting, the engineering team now wants to continuously replicate this data and consolidate these databases into a petabyte-scale data warehouse by streaming data to Amazon Redshift.</p>


<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following would you recommend as the MOST resource-efficient solution that requires the LEAST amount of development time without the need to manage the underlying infrastructure?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your answer is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-cancel"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon Kinesis Data Streams to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use AWS Glue to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use AWS EMR to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct answer</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use AWS Database Migration Service (AWS DMS) to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1009">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Use AWS Database Migration Service (AWS DMS) to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</strong></p>


<p>AWS Database Migration Service helps you migrate databases to AWS quickly and securely. The source database remains fully operational during the migration, minimizing downtime to applications that rely on the database. With AWS Database Migration Service, you can continuously replicate your data with high availability and consolidate databases into a petabyte-scale data warehouse by streaming data to Amazon Redshift and Amazon S3.</p>


<p>Continuous Data Replication
<img src="https://d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/DMS/product-page-diagram-AWS-DMS_continuous-data-replication.a0e3bd328d2a4bd9b40a83e767199dcc13cf678f.png" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/DMS/product-page-diagram-AWS-DMS_continuous-data-replication.a0e3bd328d2a4bd9b40a83e767199dcc13cf678f.png" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/dms/">https://aws.amazon.com/dms/</a></p>


<p>You can migrate data to Amazon Redshift databases using AWS Database Migration Service. Amazon Redshift is a fully managed, petabyte-scale data warehouse service in the cloud. With an Amazon Redshift database as a target, you can migrate data from all of the other supported source databases.</p>


<p>The Amazon Redshift cluster must be in the same AWS account and the same AWS Region as the replication instance.
During a database migration to Amazon Redshift, AWS DMS first moves data to an Amazon S3 bucket. When the files reside in an Amazon S3 bucket, AWS DMS then transfers them to the proper tables in the Amazon Redshift data warehouse. AWS DMS creates the S3 bucket in the same AWS Region as the Amazon Redshift database. The AWS DMS replication instance must be located in that same region.</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Use AWS Glue to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</strong> - AWS Glue is a fully managed extract, transform, and load (ETL) service that makes it easy for customers to prepare and load their data for analytics. AWS Glue job is meant to be used for batch ETL data processing.</p>


<p>Using AWS Glue involves significant development efforts to write custom migration scripts to copy the database data into Redshift.</p>


<p><strong>Use AWS EMR to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</strong> - Amazon EMR is the industry-leading cloud big data platform for processing vast amounts of data using open source tools such as Apache Spark, Apache Hive, Apache HBase, Apache Flink, Apache Hudi, and Presto. With EMR you can run Petabyte-scale analysis at less than half of the cost of traditional on-premises solutions and over 3x faster than standard Apache Spark. For short-running jobs, you can spin up and spin down clusters and pay per second for the instances used. For long-running workloads, you can create highly available clusters that automatically scale to meet demand. Amazon EMR uses Hadoop, an open-source framework, to distribute your data and processing across a resizable cluster of Amazon EC2 instances.</p>


<p>Using EMR involves significant infrastructure management efforts to set up and maintain the EMR cluster. Additionally this option involves a major development effort to write custom migration jobs to copy the database data into Redshift.</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon Kinesis Data Streams to replicate the data from the databases into Amazon Redshift</strong> - Amazon Kinesis Data Streams (KDS) is a massively scalable and durable real-time data streaming service. KDS can continuously capture gigabytes of data per second from hundreds of thousands of sources such as website clickstreams, database event streams, financial transactions, social media feeds, IT logs, and location-tracking events.</p>


<p>However, the user is expected to manually provision an appropriate number of shards to process the expected volume of the incoming data stream. The throughput of an Amazon Kinesis data stream is designed to scale without limits via increasing the number of shards within a data stream. Therefore Kinesis Data Streams is not the right fit for this use-case.</p>

<p><a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/dms/latest/userguide/CHAP_Target.Redshift.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/dms/latest/userguide/CHAP_Target.Redshift.html</a></p>

The DevOps team at the organization has set up an AWS Managed IPSec VPN Connection between their remote on-premises network and their Amazon VPC over the internet.</p>


<p>Which of the following represents the correct configuration for the IPSec VPN Connection?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the on-premises side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the AWS side of the VPN</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your answer is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the AWS side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the on-premises side of the VPN</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create a Customer Gateway on both the AWS side of the VPN as well as the on-premises side of the VPN</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on both the AWS side of the VPN as well as the on-premises side of the VPN</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1011">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the AWS side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the on-premises side of the VPN</strong></p>


<p>Amazon VPC provides the facility to create an IPsec VPN connection (also known as AWS site-to-site VPN) between remote customer networks and their Amazon VPC over the internet. The following are the key concepts for a site-to-site VPN:</p>


<p>Virtual private gateway: A virtual private gateway (VGW), also known as a VPN Gateway is the endpoint on the AWS VPC side of your VPN connection.</p>


<p>VPN connection: A secure connection between your on-premises equipment and your VPCs.</p>


<p>VPN tunnel: An encrypted link where data can pass from the customer network to or from AWS.</p>


<p>Customer Gateway: An AWS resource that provides information to AWS about your Customer Gateway device.</p>


<p>Customer Gateway device: A physical device or software application on the customer side of the Site-to-Site VPN connection.</p>


<p>AWS Managed IPSec VPN
<img src="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/whitepapers/latest/aws-vpc-connectivity-options/images/aws-managed-vpn.png" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/whitepapers/latest/aws-vpc-connectivity-options/images/aws-managed-vpn.png" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/whitepapers/latest/aws-vpc-connectivity-options/aws-managed-vpn-network-to-amazon.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/whitepapers/latest/aws-vpc-connectivity-options/aws-managed-vpn-network-to-amazon.html</a></p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the on-premises side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the AWS side of the VPN</strong> - You need to create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the AWS side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the on-premises side of the VPN. Therefore, this option is wrong.</p>


<p><strong>Create a Customer Gateway on both the AWS side of the VPN as well as the on-premises side of the VPN</strong> - You need to create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the AWS side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the on-premises side of the VPN. Therefore, this option is wrong.</p>


<p><strong>Create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on both the AWS side of the VPN as well as the on-premises side of the VPN</strong> - You need to create a virtual private gateway (VGW) on the AWS side of the VPN and a Customer Gateway on the on-premises side of the VPN. Therefore, this option is wrong.</p>

Since the application handles sensitive customer data, the security team at the company wants to ensure that any third-party Secure Sockets Layer certificate (SSL certificate) SSL/Transport Layer Security (TLS) certificates configured on Amazon EC2 instances via the AWS Certificate Manager (ACM) are renewed before their expiry date. The company has hired you as an AWS Certified Solutions Architect Associate to build a solution that notifies the security team 30 days before the certificate expiration. The solution should require the least amount of scripting and maintenance effort.</p>


<p>What will you recommend?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Monitor the <code>days to expiry</code> Amazon CloudWatch metric for certificates created via ACM. Create a CloudWatch alarm to monitor such certificates based on the <code>days to expiry</code> metric and then trigger a custom action of notifying the security team</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your answer is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-success"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Leverage AWS Config managed rule to check if any third-party SSL/TLS certificates imported into ACM are marked for expiration within 30 days. Configure the rule to trigger an Amazon SNS notification to the security team if any certificate expires within 30 days</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Leverage AWS Config managed rule to check if any SSL/TLS certificates created via ACM are marked for expiration within 30 days. Configure the rule to trigger an Amazon SNS notification to the security team if any certificate expires within 30 days</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Monitor the <code>days to expiry</code> Amazon CloudWatch metric for certificates imported into ACM. Create a CloudWatch alarm to monitor such certificates based on the <code>days to expiry</code> metric and then trigger a custom action of notifying the security team</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1013">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Leverage AWS Config managed rule to check if any third-party SSL/TLS certificates imported into ACM are marked for expiration within 30 days. Configure the rule to trigger an Amazon SNS notification to the security team if any certificate expires within 30 days</strong></p>


<p>AWS Certificate Manager is a service that lets you easily provision, manage, and deploy public and private Secure Sockets Layer/Transport Layer Security (SSL/TLS) certificates for use with AWS services and your internal connected resources. SSL/TLS certificates are used to secure network communications and establish the identity of websites over the Internet as well as resources on private networks.</p>


<p>AWS Config provides a detailed view of the configuration of AWS resources in your AWS account. This includes how the resources are related to one another and how they were configured in the past so that you can see how the configurations and relationships change over time.</p>


<p><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q9-i2.jpg" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q9-i2.jpg" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/config/latest/developerguide/how-does-config-work.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/config/latest/developerguide/how-does-config-work.html</a></p>


<p>AWS Config provides AWS-managed rules, which are predefined, customizable rules that AWS Config uses to evaluate whether your AWS resources comply with common best practices. You can leverage an AWS Config managed rule to check if any ACM certificates in your account are marked for expiration within the specified number of days. Certificates provided by ACM are automatically renewed. ACM does not automatically renew the certificates that you import. The rule is NON_COMPLIANT if your certificates are about to expire.</p>


<p><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q9-i3.jpg" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q9-i3.jpg" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/config/latest/developerguide/how-does-config-work.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/config/latest/developerguide/how-does-config-work.html</a></p>


<p>You can configure AWS Config to stream configuration changes and notifications to an Amazon SNS topic. For example, when a resource is updated, you can get a notification sent to your email, so that you can view the changes. You can also be notified when AWS Config evaluates your custom or managed rules against your resources.</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Monitor the <code>days to expiry</code> Amazon CloudWatch metric for certificates imported into ACM. Create a CloudWatch alarm to monitor such certificates based on the <code>days to expiry</code> metric and then trigger a custom action of notifying the security team</strong> - AWS Certificate Manager (ACM) does not attempt to renew third-party certificates that are imported. Also, an administrator needs to reconfigure missing DNS records for certificates that use DNS validation if the record was removed for any reason after the certificate was issued. Metrics and events provide you visibility into such certificates that require intervention to continue the renewal process. Amazon CloudWatch metrics and Amazon EventBridge events are enabled for all certificates that are managed by ACM. Users can monitor <code>days to expiry</code> as a metric for ACM certificates through Amazon CloudWatch. An Amazon EventBridge expiry event is published for any certificate that is at least 45 days away from expiry by default. Users can build alarms to monitor certificates based on days to expiry and also trigger custom actions such as calling a Lambda function or paging an administrator.</p>


<p>It is certainly possible to use the <code>days to expiry</code> CloudWatch metric to build a CloudWatch alarm to monitor the imported ACM certificates. The alarm will, in turn, trigger a notification to the security team. But this option needs more configuration effort than directly using the AWS Config managed rule that is available off-the-shelf.</p>


<p><strong>Leverage AWS Config managed rule to check if any SSL/TLS certificates created via ACM are marked for expiration within 30 days. Configure the rule to trigger an Amazon SNS notification to the security team if any certificate expires within 30 days</strong></p>


<p><strong>Monitor the <code>days to expiry</code> Amazon CloudWatch metric for certificates created via ACM. Create a CloudWatch alarm to monitor such certificates based on the <code>days to expiry</code> metric and then trigger a custom action of notifying the security team</strong></p>


<p>Any SSL/TLS certificates created via ACM do not need any monitoring/intervention for expiration. ACM automatically renews such certificates. Hence both these options are incorrect.</p>

To improve the security of these services, the Risk Advisory group has suggested a feasibility check for using the Amazon GuardDuty service.</p>


<p>Which of the following would you identify as data sources supported by Amazon GuardDuty?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div Domain Name System (DNS) logs, AWS CloudTrail events</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Amazon CloudFront logs, Amazon API Gateway logs, AWS CloudTrail events</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1015">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>VPC Flow Logs, Domain Name System (DNS) logs, AWS CloudTrail events</strong></p>


<p>Amazon GuardDuty is a threat detection service that continuously monitors for malicious activity and unauthorized behavior to protect your AWS accounts, workloads, and data stored in Amazon S3. With the cloud, the collection and aggregation of account and network activities is simplified, but it can be time-consuming for security teams to continuously analyze event log data for potential threats. With GuardDuty, you now have an intelligent and cost-effective option for continuous threat detection in AWS. The service uses machine learning, anomaly detection, and integrated threat intelligence to identify and prioritize potential threats.</p>


<p>Amazon GuardDuty analyzes tens of billions of events across multiple AWS data sources, such as AWS CloudTrail events, Amazon VPC Flow Logs, and DNS logs.</p>


<p>With a few clicks in the AWS Management Console, GuardDuty can be enabled with no software or hardware to deploy or maintain. By integrating with Amazon EventBridge Events, GuardDuty alerts are actionable, easy to aggregate across multiple accounts, and straightforward to push into existing event management and workflow systems.</p>


<p>How Amazon GuardDuty works:
<img src="https://d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/Amazon%20GuardDuty/product-page-diagram-Amazon-GuardDuty_how-it-works.a4daf7e3aaf3532623a3797dd3af606a85fc2e7b.png" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/Amazon%20GuardDuty/product-page-diagram-Amazon-GuardDuty_how-it-works.a4daf7e3aaf3532623a3797dd3af606a85fc2e7b.png" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/guardduty/">https://aws.amazon.com/guardduty/</a></p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>VPC Flow Logs, Amazon API Gateway logs, Amazon S3 access logs</strong></p>


<p><strong>Elastic Load Balancing logs, Domain Name System (DNS) logs, AWS CloudTrail events</strong></p>


<p><strong>Amazon CloudFront logs, Amazon API Gateway logs, AWS CloudTrail events</strong></p>


<p>These three options contradict the explanation provided above, so these options are incorrect.</p>


<p>Reference:</p>


<p><a href="https://aws.amazon.com/guardduty/">https://aws.amazon.com/guardduty/</a></p>
</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">Design Secure Architectures</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-wrapper--2bGiz"><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane--sIcOh result-pane--accordion-panel--TEJg7"><div class="result-pane--question-header-wrapper--3DCpC"><div class="result-pane--question-header--pTUOx"><span class="result-pane--question-header-collapsed-text--WVdEr"><span class="result-pane--pane-title--f-2kd ud-heading-md"><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon" class="result-pane--answer-status-icon--ebl6C"><span class="result-pane--question-icon-background--AskFJ" data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon-background" style="background: oklch(0.9759 0.0029 264.54);"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium" style="color: oklch(0.6671 0.2202 28.6);"><use xlink:href="#icon-error"></use></svg></span></span><span>Question 51</span><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-label" style="color: oklch(0.5573 0.2161 29.71);">Incorrect</span></span><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-large ud-btn-ghost ud-btn-text-md ud-btn-icon ud-btn-icon-large"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-collapse"></use></svg></button></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="result-pane--question-format--PBvdY ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="question-prompt"><p>You have been hired as a Solutions Architect to advise a company on the various authentication/authorization mechanisms that AWS offers to authorize an API call within the Amazon API Gateway. The company would prefer a solution that offers built-in user management.</p>


<p>Which of the following solutions would you suggest as the best fit for the given use-case?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use AWS_IAM authorization</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct answer</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon Cognito User Pools</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your answer is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-cancel"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon Cognito Identity Pools</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use AWS Lambda authorizer for Amazon API Gateway</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1017">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon Cognito User Pools</strong></p>


<p>A user pool is a user directory in Amazon Cognito. You can leverage Amazon Cognito User Pools to either provide built-in user management or integrate with external identity providers, such as Facebook, Twitter, Google+, and Amazon. Whether your users sign-in directly or through a third party, all members of the user pool have a directory profile that you can access through a Software Development Kit (SDK).</p>


<p>User pools provide:
1. Sign-up and sign-in services.
2. A built-in, customizable web UI to sign in users.
3. Social sign-in with Facebook, Google, Login with Amazon, and Sign in with Apple, as well as sign-in with SAML identity providers from your user pool.
4. User directory management and user profiles.
5. Security features such as multi-factor authentication (MFA), checks for compromised credentials, account takeover protection, and phone and email verification.
6. Customized workflows and user migration through AWS Lambda triggers.</p>


<p>After creating an Amazon Cognito user pool, in API Gateway, you must then create a COGNITO_USER_POOLS authorizer that uses the user pool.</p>


<p>Amazon Cognito User Pools:
<img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q24-i1.jpg" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt2-q24-i1.jpg" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/wellarchitected/latest/serverless-applications-lens/identity-and-access-management.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/wellarchitected/latest/serverless-applications-lens/identity-and-access-management.html</a></p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Use AWS_IAM authorization</strong> - For consumers who currently are located within your AWS environment or have the means to retrieve AWS Identity and Access Management (IAM) temporary credentials to access your environment, you can use AWS_IAM authorization and add least-privileged permissions to the respective IAM role to securely invoke your API. API Gateway API Keys is not a security mechanism and should not be used for authorization unless it’s a public API. It should be used primarily to track a consumer’s usage across your API.</p>


<p><strong>Use AWS Lambda authorizer for Amazon API Gateway</strong> - If you have an existing Identity Provider (IdP), you can use an AWS Lambda authorizer for Amazon API Gateway to invoke a Lambda function to authenticate/validate a given user against your Identity Provider. You can use a Lambda authorizer for custom validation logic based on identity metadata.</p>


<p>A Lambda authorizer can send additional information derived from a bearer token or request context values to your backend service. For example, the authorizer can return a map containing user IDs, user names, and scope. By using Lambda authorizers, your backend does not need to map authorization tokens to user-centric data, allowing you to limit the exposure of such information to just the authorization function.</p>


<p>When using Lambda authorizers, AWS strictly advises against passing credentials or any sort of sensitive data via query string parameters or headers, so this is not as secure as using Amazon Cognito User Pools.</p>


<p>In addition, both these options do not offer built-in user management.</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon Cognito Identity Pools</strong> - The two main components of Amazon Cognito are user pools and identity pools. Identity pools provide AWS credentials to grant your users access to other AWS services. To enable users in your user pool to access AWS resources, you can configure an identity pool to exchange user pool tokens for AWS credentials. So, identity pools aren't an authentication mechanism in themselves and hence aren't a choice for this use case.</p>

<p><a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/wellarchitected/latest/serverless-applications-lens/identity-and-access-management.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/wellarchitected/latest/serverless-applications-lens/identity-and-access-management.html</a></p>


<p><a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/apigateway-enable-cognito-user-pool.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/apigateway-enable-cognito-user-pool.html</a></p>


<p><a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/cognito/latest/developerguide/cognito-user-identity-pools.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/cognito/latest/developerguide/cognito-user-identity-pools.html</a></p>

The company has multiple long-term server bound licenses across the application stack and the CTO wants to continue to utilize those licenses while moving to AWS.</p>


<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following would you recommend as the MOST cost-effective solution?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct answer</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EC2 dedicated hosts</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EC2 dedicated instances</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EC2 on-demand instances</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your answer is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-cancel"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EC2 reserved instances (RI)</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1019">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EC2 dedicated hosts</strong></p>


<p>You can use Dedicated Hosts to launch Amazon EC2 instances on physical servers that are dedicated for your use. Dedicated Hosts give you additional visibility and control over how instances are placed on a physical server, and you can reliably use the same physical server over time. As a result, Dedicated Hosts enable you to use your existing server-bound software licenses like Windows Server and address corporate compliance and regulatory requirements.</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EC2 dedicated instances</strong> - Dedicated instances are Amazon EC2 instances that run in a VPC on hardware that's dedicated to a single customer. Your dedicated instances are physically isolated at the host hardware level from instances that belong to other AWS accounts. Dedicated instances may share hardware with other instances from the same AWS account that are not dedicated instances. Dedicated instances cannot be used for existing server-bound software licenses.</p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EC2 on-demand instances</strong></p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EC2 reserved instances (RI)</strong></p>


<p>Amazon EC2 presents a virtual computing environment, allowing you to use web service interfaces to launch instances with a variety of operating systems, load them with your custom application environment, manage your network’s access permissions, and run your image using as many or few systems as you desire.</p>


<p>Amazon EC2 provides the following purchasing options to enable you to optimize your costs based on your needs:</p>


<p>On-Demand Instances – Pay, by the second, for the instances that you launch.</p>


<p>Reserved Instances (RI) – Reduce your Amazon EC2 costs by making a commitment to a consistent instance configuration, including instance type and Region, for a term of 1 or 3 years.</p>


<p>Neither on-demand instances nor reserved instances can be used for existing server-bound software licenses.</p>

The team wants to use either a Network Address Translation (NAT) instance or a Network Address Translation (NAT) gateway in the public subnet to enable instances in the private subnet to initiate outbound IPv4 traffic to the internet but needs some technical assistance in terms of the configuration options available for the Network Address Translation (NAT) instance and the Network Address Translation (NAT) gateway.</p>


<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following options would you identify as CORRECT? (Select three)</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your selection is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-filled"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>NAT instance can be used as a bastion server</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-checkbox-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>NAT gateway can be used as a bastion server</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); <p><strong>NAT instance can be used as a bastion server</strong></p>


<p><strong>Security Groups can be associated with a NAT instance</strong></p>


<p><strong>NAT instance supports port forwarding</strong></p>


<p>A NAT instance or a NAT Gateway can be used in a public subnet in your VPC to enable instances in the private subnet to initiate outbound IPv4 traffic to the Internet.</p>

<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following steps would you recommend?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your answer is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-cancel"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Both IAM roles and IAM users can be used interchangeably for cross-account access</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct answer</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create a new IAM role with the required permissions to access the resources in the production environment. The users can then assume this IAM role while accessing the resources from the production environment</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>It is not possible to access cross-account resources</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Create new IAM user credentials for the production environment and share these credentials with the set of users from the development environment</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1023">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Create a new IAM role with the required permissions to access the resources in the production environment. The users can then assume this IAM role while accessing the resources from the production environment</strong></p>


<p>IAM roles allow you to delegate access to users or services that normally don't have access to your organization's AWS resources. IAM users or AWS services can assume a role to obtain temporary security credentials that can be used to make AWS API calls. Consequently, you don't have to share long-term credentials for access to a resource. Using IAM roles, it is possible to access cross-account resources.</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Create new IAM user credentials for the production environment and share these credentials with the set of users from the development environment</strong> - There is no need to create new IAM user credentials for the production environment, as you can use IAM roles to access cross-account resources.</p>


<p><strong>It is not possible to access cross-account resources</strong> - You can use IAM roles to access cross-account resources.</p>


<p><strong>Both IAM roles and IAM users can be used interchangeably for cross-account access</strong> - IAM roles and IAM users are separate IAM entities and should not be mixed. Only IAM roles can be used to access cross-account resources.</p>


<p>Reference:</p>


<p><a href="https://aws.amazon.com/iam/features/manage-roles/">https://aws.amazon.com/iam/features/manage-roles/</a></p>

The company needs 15 Amazon EC2 instances for optimal performance.</p>


<p>How many Availability Zones (AZs) will the company need to deploy these Amazon EC2 instances per the given use-case?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your answer is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg
