</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">Design High-Performing Architectures</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-wrapper--2bGiz"><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane--sIcOh result-pane--accordion-panel--TEJg7"><div class="result-pane--question-header-wrapper--3DCpC"><div class="result-pane--question-header--pTUOx"><span class="result-pane--question-header-collapsed-text--WVdEr"><span class="result-pane--pane-title--f-2kd ud-heading-md"><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon" class="result-pane--answer-status-icon--ebl6C"><span class="result-pane--question-icon-background--AskFJ" data-purpose="question-result-header-status-icon-background" style="background: oklch(0.9759 0.0029 264.54);"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium" style="color: oklch(0.6459 0.1519 154.89);"><use xlink:href="#icon-success"></use></svg></span></span><span>Question 64</span><span data-purpose="question-result-header-status-label" style="color: oklch(0.4449 0.0863 157.92);">Correct</span></span><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-large ud-btn-ghost ud-btn-text-md ud-btn-icon ud-btn-icon-large"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-medium ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-collapse"></use></svg></button></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="result-pane--question-format--PBvdY ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="question-prompt"><p>A big data analytics company is using Amazon Kinesis Data Streams (KDS) to process IoT data from the field devices of an agricultural sciences company. Multiple consumer applications are using the incoming data streams and the engineers have noticed a performance lag for the data delivery speed between producers and consumers of the data streams.</p>


<p>As a solutions architect, which of the following would you recommend for improving the performance for the given use-case?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon SQS Standard queues</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon SQS FIFO queues</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Your answer is correct</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-success"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Enhanced Fanout feature of Amazon Kinesis Data Streams</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1043">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Use Enhanced Fanout feature of Amazon Kinesis Data Streams</strong></p>


<p>Amazon Kinesis Data Streams (KDS) is a massively scalable and durable real-time data streaming service. KDS can continuously capture gigabytes of data per second from hundreds of thousands of sources such as website clickstreams, database event streams, financial transactions, social media feeds, IT logs, and location-tracking events.</p>


<p>By default, the 2MB/second/shard output is shared between all of the applications consuming data from the stream. You should use enhanced fan-out if you have multiple consumers retrieving data from a stream in parallel. With enhanced fan-out developers can register stream consumers to use enhanced fan-out and receive their own 2MB/second pipe of read throughput per shard, and this throughput automatically scales with the number of shards in a stream.</p>


<p>Amazon Kinesis Data Streams Fanout:
<img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt5-q38-i1.jpg" style="display: none;"><span class="ud-component--base-components--open-full-size-image"><div class="open-full-size-image--wrapper--R4gIm" data-purpose="open-full-size-image"><img src="https://assets-pt.media.datacumulus.com/aws-saa-pt/assets/pt5-q38-i1.jpg" alt="" loading="eager"><button type="button" class="ud-btn ud-btn-medium ud-btn-link ud-btn-text-sm open-full-size-image--backdrop--Zor3j"><svg aria-label="Larger image" role="img" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-large ud-icon-color-neutral"><use xlink:href="#icon-search"></use></svg></button></div></span>
via - <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/blogs/aws/kds-enhanced-fanout/">https://aws.amazon.com/blogs/aws/kds-enhanced-fanout/</a></p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose</strong> -  Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose is the easiest way to reliably load streaming data into data lakes, data stores, and analytics tools. It is a fully managed service that automatically scales to match the throughput of your data and requires no ongoing administration. It can also batch, compress, transform, and encrypt the data before loading it, minimizing the amount of storage used at the destination and increasing security. Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose can only write to Amazon S3, Amazon Redshift, Amazon Elasticsearch or Splunk. You can't have applications consuming data streams from Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose, that's the job of Amazon Kinesis Data Streams. Therefore this option is not correct.</p>


<p><strong>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon SQS Standard queues</strong></p>


<p><strong>Swap out Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Amazon SQS FIFO queues</strong></p>


<p>Amazon Simple Queue Service (Amazon SQS) is a fully managed message queuing service that enables you to decouple and scale microservices, distributed systems, and serverless applications. Amazon SQS offers two types of message queues. Standard queues offer maximum throughput, best-effort ordering, and at-least-once delivery. Amazon SQS FIFO queues are designed to guarantee that messages are processed exactly once, in the exact order that they are sent. As multiple applications are consuming the same stream concurrently, both Amazon SQS Standard and Amazon SQS FIFO are not the right fit for the given use-case.</p>


<p>Exam Alert:</p>


<p>Please understand the differences between the capabilities of Amazon Kinesis Data Streams vs Amazon SQS, as you may be asked scenario-based questions on this topic in the exam.</p>

Because of an unknown bug, the application causes the instance to freeze regularly. Then, the instance has to be manually restarted via the AWS management console.</p>


<p>Which of the following is the MOST cost-optimal and resource-efficient way to implement an automated solution until a permanent fix is delivered by the development team?</p></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-result-pane-expanded-content--Og5Vc"><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EventBridge events to trigger an AWS Lambda function to check the instance status every 5 minutes. In the case of Instance Health Check failure, the AWS lambda function can use Amazon EC2 API to reboot the instance</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-correct--PLOEU" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8101 0.0873 162.22); color: oklch(0.3072 0.0555 158.67);">Correct answer</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Setup an Amazon CloudWatch alarm to monitor the health status of the instance. In case of an Instance Health Check failure, an EC2 Reboot CloudWatch Alarm Action can be used to reboot the instance</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-incorrect--vFyOv" data-purpose="answer"><div><span data-purpose="answer-result-header-user-label" class="result-pane--answer-by-user-label--PSH86 ud-heading-xs" style="background: oklch(0.8453 0.0845 23.47); color: oklch(0.4224 0.1681 30.2666);">Your answer is incorrect</span></div><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.2565 0.0265 278.04);"><use xlink:href="#icon-cancel"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Setup an Amazon CloudWatch alarm to monitor the health status of the instance. In case of an Instance Health Check failure, Amazon CloudWatch Alarm can publish to an Amazon Simple Notification Service (Amazon SNS) event which can then trigger an AWS lambda function. The AWS lambda function can use Amazon EC2 API to reboot the instance</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--answer-result-pane--Niazi"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-skipped--1NDPn" data-purpose="answer"><div class="answer-result-pane--answer-body--cDGY6" data-purpose="answer-body"><span data-purpose="answer-result-body-selection-icon" class="answer-result-pane--answer-selection-icon--O6Xkn"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="ud-icon ud-icon-small" style="color: oklch(0.6722 0.0355 279.77);"><use xlink:href="#icon-radio-empty"></use></svg></span><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-heading-md rt-scaffolding" id="answer-text"><p>Use Amazon EventBridge events to trigger an AWS Lambda function to reboot the instance status every 5 minutes</p></div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1045">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation"><p>Correct option:</p>


<p><strong>Setup an Amazon CloudWatch alarm to monitor the health status of the instance. In case of an Instance Health Check failure, an EC2 Reboot CloudWatch Alarm Action can be used to reboot the instance</strong></p>


<p>Using Amazon CloudWatch alarm actions, you can create alarms that automatically stop, terminate, reboot, or recover your Amazon EC2 instances. You can use the stop or terminate actions to help you save money when you no longer need an instance to be running. You can use the reboot and recover actions to automatically reboot those instances or recover them onto new hardware if a system impairment occurs.</p>


<p>You can create an Amazon CloudWatch alarm that monitors an Amazon EC2 instance and automatically reboots the instance. The reboot alarm action is recommended for Instance Health Check failures (as opposed to the recover alarm action, which is suited for System Health Check failures).</p>


<p>Incorrect options:</p>


<p><strong>Setup an Amazon CloudWatch alarm to monitor the health status of the instance. In case of an Instance Health Check failure, Amazon CloudWatch Alarm can publish to an Amazon Simple Notification Service (Amazon SNS) event which can then trigger an AWS lambda function. The AWS lambda function can use Amazon EC2 API to reboot the instance</strong></p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EventBridge events to trigger an AWS Lambda function to check the instance status every 5 minutes. In the case of Instance Health Check failure, the AWS lambda function can use Amazon EC2 API to reboot the instance</strong></p>


<p><strong>Use Amazon EventBridge events to trigger an AWS Lambda function to reboot the instance status every 5 minutes</strong></p>


<p>Using Amazon EventBridge event or Amazon CloudWatch alarm to trigger an AWS lambda function, directly or indirectly, is wasteful of resources. You should just use the EC2 Reboot CloudWatch Alarm Action to reboot the instance. So all the options that trigger the AWS lambda function are incorrect.</p>


<p>Reference:</p>


<p><a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonCloudWatch/latest/monitoring/UsingAlarmActions.html">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonCloudWatch/latest/monitoring/UsingAlarmActions.html</a></p>
